# ep01_prompts — 《왜 졌는지 말해봐》 EP01 v2 **패널 프롬프트 56** (2026-07-13 · prompt-smith)

입력: `04_visual/ep01_shotlist.md`(56패널) · `04_visual/ep01_lettering.md`(말풍선 59 + 화면 라벨 20) · `04_visual/style-bible.md`(v3 §1·§2·§4·§5-A·§5-B·§5-C·§6·§8) · `04_visual/character-sheets.md` · `02_story/characters.md`(표정 27컷)

소비자: `_split_prompts.py` → `_render_jobs/panels/*.txt` · `_make_refs.py`(← `04_visual/ep01_refs_map.tsv`) → `*.refs` · **panel-artist-a/b/c**(REGEN) · **panel-validator**(C1~C6)


> ## ⛔⛔ negative 규약 (v1은 여기서 죽었다)
> **`no text` · `no korean text` · `no letters` · `no writing` · `no numbers` · `no digits`를 negative에 쓰지 않았다 — 0건.**
> 넣는 순간 말풍선 59개와 반전 라벨(`시야 없음`·`전력분석관`)이 전부 사라진다.
> 숫자 차단은 **화면 안으로만 한정**(`no legible numbers on the game screen …`) — **P04의 `고3`(숫자 3)이 살아야 하기 때문이다.**
>
> ## ★ 모든 패널에 ACTING 블록이 있다 (56/56)
> 레퍼런스 시트를 `-i`로 첨부하면 **카탈로그 미소·반짝이는 눈이 복사된다.** ACTING은 시트의 **얼굴을 덮어쓴다**(몸·외형은 시트가 정본).
> ⛔ **덮어쓰기이지 지우기가 아니다** — **H7·H9·R7·O9는 미소가 정답**이라 프롬프트가 미소를 *요구*한다. **무표정 = 1급 REGEN.**
>
> ## 형식
> 헤더는 `### panel_NNN`, 프롬프트는 **`- prompt: "…"` 한 줄**(`_split_prompts.py` 파서 규격 — `^###\s+panel_(\d{3})` + `^\s*-\s*prompt:\s*"`).


---


## ▣ SC01 · `LOC_LOBBY` · WARM_DAY

### panel_001
- scene_group: A
- scene_id: SC01 / location: LOC_LOBBY / light: WARM_DAY / ratio: B
- refs: 04_visual/refs/Hanji_ref.png
- prompt: "STYLE: korean webtoon panel, warm cozy lo-fi anime illustration, ONE UNIFIED DRAWING LANGUAGE for characters AND background - everything in the frame is drawn by the same hand; chibi animal characters (2-3 heads tall) with bold clean black ink outlines, crisp cel shading with one soft gradient pass, large round eyes with bright highlights; the ENVIRONMENT IS DRAWN IN THE SAME CEL-SHADED INK STYLE: simplified rounded props with softened corners, chunky friendly shapes, clean flat color fills, and VISIBLE INK OUTLINES ON ALL FURNITURE AND OBJECTS (slightly thinner than the character outlines but the same black ink); accurate perspective, real esports gear kept recognizable but drawn simply; furniture and peripherals are scaled to the chibi bodies; cozy warm lighting with a warm light source in frame, indigo and violet shadows instead of black, glowing screens with soft bloom; bright saturated colors, inviting cozy atmosphere; NO photographic texture, NO material grain, NO photo lighting; no fantasy elements. LOC_LOBBY: bright welcoming esports academy lobby drawn in warm cel-shaded anime style, a tall glass front wall with GOLDEN AFTERNOON SUNLIGHT pouring in and laying warm rectangles of light across a warm wooden floor, creamy white walls, one rounded sofa with a low round table, a single potted plant with simple rounded leaves, a blank standing banner with NO text on it, a clean wall plaque mounted on the wall; simplified rounded props with clean black ink outlines and flat cel fills, gentle peach-tinted shadows, soft bloom around the sunlight, airy cheerful and warm; NO photo texture, NO signage other than the wall plaque, NO logos, NO price lists. WARM_DAY: warm bright lighting - creamy warm-white ceiling light, soft golden afternoon daylight through the blinds, warm wood and cream surfaces, gentle peach-tinted shadows, airy and clean; high key and cheerful, absolutely not clinical, not blue-gray, not a cold office. REFERENCE ANCHOR: match the exact appearance of HANJI (locked reference sheet: 04_visual/refs/Hanji_ref.png) - the attached reference sheet(s) define the BODY, colours and outfit exactly; the FACE and expression are defined by the ACTING block below, which OVERRIDES the sheet's catalog pose, catalog smile and sparkling catalog eyes. CHARACTER TOKENS: HANJI = penguin boy, navy-black back and head, white belly front, short rounded orange beak, a single strand of feather sticking up from the crown, large round AMBER eyes, TEAL headset with a boom mic, orange webbed feet, short mitten flippers for arms (NEVER feathered wings), 2.5-head chibi proportions, bold black ink outline, clean cel shading; he is taller than RAKU by one head and smaller than HOO. CAMERA/COMPOSITION: wide straight-on establishing shot of the lobby. Golden afternoon sunlight pours through the tall glass front wall and lays warm rectangles of light across the warm wooden floor. HANJI has just stepped one foot through the glass door and STOPPED - he stands small in the RIGHT THIRD of the frame, three-quarter front view, his FACE DRAWN LARGE ENOUGH TO READ CLEARLY (⛔ no silhouette, no back of the head). On the upper-LEFT cream wall the clean WALL PLAQUE hangs facing the camera, large and unobstructed. ACTING (this OVERRIDES the reference sheet's catalog pose and catalog smile - the sheet defines the BODY and outfit, this defines the FACE): H1 (anxious arrival) - eyelids half lowered, gaze cast down at 45 degrees ; inner ends of the eyebrows pushed up into a worried slant ; beak CLOSED and angled slightly down ; shoulders pulled in, head slightly bowed ; the single crown feather droops limply. His expression must clearly read as NERVOUS at a glance, even with the balloon covered. NO SMILE - anxious. SCREEN TEXT: the wall plaque carries the EXACT Korean text \"농심 이스포츠 아카데미\" in heavy BLACK gothic sans-serif on the bright plaque, LARGE, correctly spelled and CLEARLY LEGIBLE (do not draw the quotation marks). ⛔ no other signage, no logos, no english, no numbers anywhere in the frame; the standing banner stays completely blank. LETTERING: speech balloons and Korean text are DRAWN INTO THE ARTWORK with the same black ink as the characters - white rounded balloon with a BOLD BLACK INK OUTLINE (same weight as the character outline) and a triangular tail pointing at the speaker's beak; the Korean text is HEAVY GOTHIC SANS-SERIF, black, horizontal, high contrast, LARGE and clearly legible, generous padding inside the balloon; balloons stay WHITE even in the dim analysis room; the lettering is part of the drawing, NOT a flat pasted digital font layer; the quotation marks themselves are NOT drawn ONE speech balloon: a white rounded balloon with a bold black ink tail pointing at HANJI's beak, placed in the UPPER-RIGHT margin just above and right of his head, containing the EXACT Korean text \"아, 여기 맞나…\" on one line. ⛔ the balloon must NOT touch or cover the wall plaque on the upper LEFT. OUTPUT FORMAT: horizontal wide panel, aspect ratio 3:2, 1536x1024 pixels, full-bleed webtoon panel. negative: no photorealistic background, no photographic texture, no photo lighting, no realistic office render, no live-action background, no 3d render, no CG background, no photobash, no photograph, no hyperdetailed environment, no material grain, no film grain, no lens flare, no light leaks, no bokeh circles, no chromatic aberration, no HDR, no gritty, no grime, no dirt, no rust, no stains, no scratched surfaces, no macro fingerprints, no mismatched art styles, no character pasted onto a realistic background, no unlined background, no gloomy, no grim, no bleak, no oppressive, no desaturated, no muted colors, no cold gray palette, no clinical office lighting, no black shadows, no pitch black darkness, no black fog overlay, no grey fog overlay, no deadpan faces, no expressionless faces, no blank stare, no flat affect, no catalog smile, no watermark, no signature, no artist logo, no brand marks, no english text, no latin letters, no gibberish text, no garbled text, no garbled hangul, no misspelled korean, no random letters on props, no vertical text, no handwriting font, no decorative font, no colored or gradient letters, no thought bubble, no narration box, no sound effect text, no reading order arrows, no flat pasted digital font, no sticker-like text layer, no vector overlay look, no real-game UI, no copyrighted champions, no existing game logos, no champion portraits, no fantasy, no magic, no system window, no status window, no water, no ocean, no sky, no snow field, no forest, no nest, no spread feathered wings, no flying, no glasses on HANJI, no green eyes on HANJI or HOO, no teal or cyan accents on RAKU's or HOO's props, no tape patch on HOO's or HANJI's headset, no white sticker outline, no die-cut border, no reference sheet layout, no turnaround, no multiple views, no character lineup, no white studio background, no realistic animal anatomy, no crowd faces, no new characters, no glitch, no scanlines, no pixel noise, no price list, no curriculum text, no arrows, no highlight circles, no laser pointer."
- output: 05_panels/ep01/panel_001.png

His expression must clearly read as COCKY at a glance. A SMIRK, not a friendly smile. RAKU sits leaned back on the sofa with his back half turned to HANJI and rolls only his eyes to scan him from TOP to BOTTOM. RAKU is the subject: eye level, three-quarter angle, bust framing, his face fully readable. HANJI appears in the LEFT FOREGROUND as the BACK of his head and one shoulder only (still drawn with the same crisp ink line, not blurred out). ACTING (this OVERRIDES the reference sheet's catalog pose and catalog smile - the sheet defines the BODY and outfit, this defines the FACE): RAKU R1 turning into R2 (condescending) - half-lidded eyes scanning DOWNWARD from head to toe ; both eyebrows slightly raised ; mouth slanted into a half smile ; HEAD TILTED SIDEWAYS as he scans up and down ; tail lazy. His expression must clearly read as SIZING SOMEONE UP at a glance. A SMIRK - condescending scan. NOT a friendly smile. LETTERING: speech balloons and Korean text are DRAWN INTO THE ARTWORK with the same black ink as the characters - white rounded balloon with a BOLD BLACK INK OUTLINE (same weight as the character outline) and a triangular tail pointing at the speaker's beak; the Korean text is HEAVY GOTHIC SANS-SERIF, black, horizontal, high contrast, LARGE and clearly legible, generous padding inside the balloon; balloons stay WHITE even in the dim analysis room; the lettering is part of the drawing, NOT a flat pasted digital font layer; the quotation marks themselves are NOT drawn ONE speech balloon: white rounded balloon with a tail pointing at RAKU's mouth, placed UPPER-RIGHT of the frame (this exact balloon position is reused in the mirrored panel later), containing the EXACT Korean text \"…체험 수업 온 거예요?\" on one line. ### panel_004
- scene_group: A
- scene_id: SC01 / location: LOC_LOBBY / light: WARM_DAY / ratio: A
- refs: 04_visual/refs/Raku_ref.png, 04_visual/refs/Hanji_ref.png
- prompt: "STYLE: korean webtoon panel, warm cozy lo-fi anime illustration, ONE UNIFIED DRAWING LANGUAGE for characters AND background - everything in the frame is drawn by the same hand; chibi animal characters (2-3 heads tall) with bold clean black ink outlines, crisp cel shading with one soft gradient pass, large round eyes with bright highlights; the ENVIRONMENT IS DRAWN IN THE SAME CEL-SHADED INK STYLE: simplified rounded props with softened corners, chunky friendly shapes, clean flat color fills, and VISIBLE INK OUTLINES ON ALL FURNITURE AND OBJECTS (slightly thinner than the character outlines but the same black ink); accurate perspective, real esports gear kept recognizable but drawn simply; furniture and peripherals are scaled to the chibi bodies; cozy warm lighting with a warm light source in frame, indigo and violet shadows instead of black, glowing screens with soft bloom; bright saturated colors, inviting cozy atmosphere; NO photographic texture, NO material grain, NO photo lighting; no fantasy elements. CHARACTER TOKENS: RAKU = raccoon boy, grey fur, black bandit mask marking around the eyes, GREEN eyes, RED headset with a beige tape patch on the earcup, grey hoodie, lanyard ID badge, bushy ringed striped tail, the SMALLEST of the three, 2.5-head chibi proportions, bold black ink outline, clean cel shading | HANJI = penguin boy, navy-black back and head, white belly front, short rounded orange beak, a single strand of feather sticking up from the crown, large round AMBER eyes, TEAL headset with a boom mic, orange webbed feet, short mitten flippers for arms (NEVER feathered wings), 2.5-head chibi proportions, bold black ink outline, clean cel shading; he is taller than RAKU by one head and smaller than HOO. CAMERA/COMPOSITION: TWO-SHOT. RAKU seated on the sofa at lower-left, HANJI standing frozen at upper-right. BOTH FACES ARE CLEARLY READABLE in the same frame, no silhouettes. ACTING (this OVERRIDES the reference sheet's catalog pose and catalog smile - the sheet defines the BODY and outfit, this defines the FACE): RAKU R2 (looking down on him) - eye corners lowered, scanning downward ; both eyebrows slightly up ; mouth slanted into a half smile ; head tilted sideways. HANJI H2 (stung) - eyes widen slightly and the gaze SLIDES AWAY to the side ; one eyebrow up ; beak pressed into a short flat line ; head turned 15 degrees away, one mitten flipper creeping to the back of his neck ; crown feather wilting. RAKU: a SMIRK. HANJI: NO SMILE - stung, looking away. Both expressions must be nameable at a glance. LETTERING: speech balloons and Korean text are DRAWN INTO THE ARTWORK with the same black ink as the characters - white rounded balloon with a BOLD BLACK INK OUTLINE (same weight as the character outline) and a triangular tail pointing at the speaker's beak; the Korean text is HEAVY GOTHIC SANS-SERIF, black, horizontal, high contrast, LARGE and clearly legible, generous padding inside the balloon; balloons stay WHITE even in the dim analysis room; the lettering is part of the drawing, NOT a flat pasted digital font layer; the quotation marks themselves are NOT drawn ONE speech balloon: white rounded balloon, tail pointing at RAKU, placed TOP-CENTRE in the empty space between the two faces, containing the EXACT Korean text \"형 고3이면… 좀 늦지 않았어요?\" set on 2 lines - line 1 \"형 고3이면…\" and line 2 \"좀 늦지 않았어요?\". ALL characters in the balloon are the SAME size and weight - NO emphasis on any word. The characters 고3 (with the digit 3) must be rendered correctly inside the balloon. ⛔ the balloon must not cover HANJI's averted eyes. OUTPUT FORMAT: vertical portrait panel, aspect ratio 2:3, 1024x1536 pixels, full-bleed webtoon panel. negative: no photorealistic background, no photographic texture, no photo lighting, no realistic office render, no live-action background, no 3d render, no CG background, no photobash, no photograph, no hyperdetailed environment, no material grain, no film grain, no lens flare, no light leaks, no
